 Upcoming April 18 is 'akshaya-tritiya'
 jaisaa ki naam se spasht he akshay arthath jiskaa kabhi kshay naa ho
 'akshaya-tritiya' is a very important festival
 'akshay-tritiya' ko abujh va swayan siddh muhoort kii manyata praapt he
 Every year the festival of akshaya-tritiya is celebrated on Tritiya Tithi of Vaishakh Shukla Paksha
 is baar 'akshay-tritiya' 18 april ko kritika nakshatra evam sarvaarth siddhi yoga main rahegi jo bahut hi durlabh va shubh sanyog he
 The spiritual practices and donations performed on the day of Akshaya Tritiya are fruitful and remain fruitful
 'akshay-tritiya' ke din sadhak hatthajodi siddhi, lakshmi prapti sadhana, arishth nivaaran sadhana sampann kar laabh praapt kar sakate hai
 'akshat-tritiya' is a very good opportunity to get rid of Pitra-dosha, on this day, donations made for the ancestors are renewable and appease the ancestors
 akshay tritiya ke din bhuulakar bhi naa karen ye kayeekshay tritiya ke din kya karen :-1
 Happiness peace: Tie the 11 Gomti Chakras in red silk cloth and keep them in a place of worship in a silver box, always maintains an atmosphere of happiness and peace in the house
 2
 Business Benefits: By tying 27 Gomti Chakras in yellow or red silk cloth to the main gate of your establishment, there is an immediate benefit in business
 3
 Karmakshetra: If there are hurdles in the Karmakshetra or there is hindrance in promotion, then it is beneficial to offer 13 Gomti Chakras on the Shiva lingam in the pagoda on the day of 'akshaya-tritiya', remembering your wishes
 4
 Bhagyodaya: For Bhagyoday, on the day of 'akshaya-tritiya', as soon as the morning arises, first grind the 11 Gomti Chakras and make them powder, then spread this powder in front of the main door of your house remembering your God
 is prayog se kuch hi dinon main sadhak kaa durbhaagya samaapt hokar bhagyoday hota he
 To get rid of Pitra-dosha: Those who have 'pitra-dosha' in their birth chart, on the day of 'akshaya-tritiya', in the morning, on a clean place or temple, on their peoples, homemade confectionery and one Keep pure water in the pot
 pipal ke neeche dhoop-deep prajjwalit kar apane pitruganon kii santushti ke liye prarthana karen
 After that, without looking back, come straight back to your home, keep in mind that while doing this experiment, no other person's eyesight gets noticed
 is prayog ko karne se pitrugan sheeghra hi santusht hokar apana aashirwad pradaan karte hai

 dark sarkal dur karne ke liye tamaato sabase kargar upaay he

 2
 Potatoes can also be used to remove dark circles

 P

 washington vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakartaaon sang cambridge vishvavidhyalay ke shodhakartaaon ne pratyaropit hriday-koshikaon ko adhik samay tak jivit rakhane main madad karne ke liye maanav stem koshikaon se viksit hui sahaayak epicardial koshikaon kaa prayog kiya
 Researchers used 3D human heart tissue from lab-grown human stem cells to test cell combinations, finding that the supporting epicardial cells help the heart muscle cells to grow and mature
 cambridge vishvavidhyalay ke e british heart foundation (bichaef) ke shodhakarta or is shodh ke pramukh sanjay sinha ne kaha, "britain main hajaaron kii taadaat main log dil kii bimariyon ke saath ji rahe hai, inamen se kai jivan rakshak heart transplant yaa dil kaa pratyaropan karaane kii daud main hai, lekin britain main har saal keval 200 hi dil pratyaropit kiye gaye, is vajah se yah jaruri he ki ham iske vaikalpik upachaar kii khoj shuru karen
 "researchers hope that by using the cells of a patient, they will one day be able to use the power of stem cells to treat a human heart
